Header not set\")\n   355→\t\treturn req\n   356→\t}\n   357→\n   358→\ttenantids := md.Get(\"tenantid\")\n   359→\tif len(tenantids) == 0 {\n   360→\t\t// We assume we are not using multi-tenant mode, which is fine\n   361→\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Tenant ID not present. Header not set\")\n   362→\t} else if len(tenantids) > 1 {\n   363→\t\t// Loki supports multiple tenant IDs, but we should receive them from different contexts\n   364→\t\tlogger.Error(strconv.Itoa(len(tenantids)) + \" tenant IDs found. Header not set\")\n   365→\t} else {\n   366→\t\treq.Header.Add(\"X-Scope-OrgID\", tenantids[0])\n   367→\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Tenant ID \" + tenantids[0] + \" added to Loki request\")\n   368→\t}\n   369→\treturn req\n   370→}\n   371→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. readLokiError(body io.ReadCloser) error {\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\t_, err := buf.ReadFrom(body)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tbytes := buf.Bytes()\n\n\t// the error-message is versions.\n\t// so our approach is this:\n\t// - we try to convert the bytes to JSON\n\t// - we take the value of the field \"message\"\n\t// - if any of these steps fail, or if \"message\" is empty, we return the whole text\n\n\treturn makeLokiError(bytes)\n}\n\nfunc (api *LokiAPI) DataQuery(ctx context.Context, query lokiQuery, responseOpts ResponseOpts) (*backend.DataResponse, error) {\n\treq, err := makeDataRequest(ctx, api.url, query)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tqueryAttrs := []any{\"start\", query.Start, \"end\", query.End, \"step\", query.Step, \"query\", query.Expr, \"queryType\", query.QueryType, \"direction\", query.Direction, \"maxLines\", query.MaxLines, \"supportingQueryType\", query.SupportingQueryType, \"lokiHost\", req.URL.Host, \"lokiPath\", req.URL.Path}\n\tapi.log.Debug(\"Sending query to loki\", queryAttrs...)\n\tstart := time.Now()\n\tresp, err := api.client.Do(req)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tstatus := \"error\"\n\t\tif errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n\t\t\tstatus = \"cancelled\"\n\t\t}\n\t\tlp := []any{\"error\", err, \"status\", status, \"duration\", time.Since(start), \"stage\", stageDatabaseRequest}\n\t\tlp = append(lp, queryAttrs...)\n\t\tif resp != nil {\n\t\t\tlp = append(lp, \"statusCode\", resp.StatusCode)\n\t\t}\n\t\tapi.log.Debug(\"Error received from Loki\", lp...)\n\t\tif backend.IsDownstreamHTTPError(err) {\n\t\t\terr = backend.DownstreamError(err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tres := backend.ErrorResponseWithErrorSource(err)\n\t\treturn &res, nil\n\t}\n\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif err := resp.Body.Close(); err != nil {\n\t\t\tapi.log.Warn(\"Failed to close response body\", \"error\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tlp := []any{\"duration\", time.Since(start), \"stage\", stageDatabaseRequest, \"statusCode\", resp.StatusCode, \"contentLength\", resp.Header.Get(\"Content-Length\")}\n\tlp = append(lp, queryAttrs...)\n\tif resp.StatusCode/100 != 2 {\n\t\terr := readLokiError(resp.Body)\n\t\tres := backend.DataResponse{\n\t\t\tError:       err,\n\t\t\tErrorSource: backend.ErrorSourceFromHTTPStatus(resp.StatusCode),\n\t\t}\n\t\tlp = append(lp, \"status\", \"error\", \"error\", err, \"statusSource\", res.ErrorSource)\n\t\tapi.log.Debug(\"Error received from Loki\", lp...)\n\t\treturn &res, nil\n\t} else {\n\t\tlp = append(lp, \"status\", \"ok\")\n\t\tapi.log.Info(\"Response received from loki\", lp...)\n\t}\n\n\tstart = time.Now()\n\t_, span := api.tracer.Start(ctx, \"datasource.loki.parseResponse\")\n\tdefer span.End()\n\n\titer := jsoniter.Parse(jsoniter.ConfigDefault, resp.Body, 1024)\n\tres := converter.ReadPrometheusStyleResult(iter, converter.Options{})\n\n\tif res.Error != nil {\n\t\tspan.RecordError(res.Error)\n\t\tspan.SetStatus(codes.Error, res.Error.Error())\n\t\tinstrumentation.UpdatePluginParsingResponseDurationSeconds(ctx, time.Since(start), \"error\")\n\t\tapi.log.Debug(\"Error parsing response from loki\", \"error\", res.Error, \"duration\", time.Since(start), \"stage\", stageParseResponse)\n\t\treturn nil, res.Error\n\t}\n\tinstrumentation.UpdatePluginParsingResponseDurationSeconds(ctx, time.Since(start), \"ok\")\n\tapi.log.Info(\"Response parsed from loki\", \"duration\", time.Since(start), \"framesLength\", len(res.Frames), \"stage\", stageParseResponse)\n\n\treturn &res, nil\n}\n\nfunc makeRawRequest(ctx context.Context, lokiDsUrl string, resourcePath string) (*http.Request, error) {\n\tlokiUrl, err := url.Parse(lokiDsUrl)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tresourceUrl, err := url.Parse(resourcePath)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\t// we take the path and the query-string only\n\tlokiUrl.RawQuery = resourceUrl.RawQuery\n\tlokiUrl.Path = path.Join(lokiUrl.Path, resourceUrl.Path)\n\n\treq, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, \"GET\", lokiUrl.String(), nil)\n\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tsetXScopeOrgIDHeader(req, ctx)\n\n\treturn req, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *LokiAPI) RawQuery(ctx context.Context, resourcePath string) (RawLokiResponse, error) {\n\tapi.log.Debug(\"Sending raw query to loki\", \"resourcePath\", resourcePath)\n\treq, err := makeRawRequest(ctx, api.url, resourcePath)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tapi.log.Debug(\"Failed to prepare request to loki\", \"error\", err, \"resourcePath\", resourcePath)\n\t\treturn RawLokiResponse{}, err\n\t}\n\tstart := time.Now()\n\tresp, err := api.client.Do(req)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tstatus := \"error\"\n\t\tif errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n\t\t\tstatus = \"cancelled\"\n\t\t}\n\t\tlp := []any{\"error\", err, \"resourcePath\", resourcePath, \"status\", status, \"duration\", time.Since(start), \"stage\", stageDatabaseRequest}\n\t\tif resp != nil {\n\t\t\tlp = append(lp, \"statusCode\", resp.StatusCode)\n\t\t}\n\t\tapi.log.Debug(\"Error received from Loki\", lp...)\n\t\treturn RawLokiResponse{}, err\n\t}\n\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif err := resp.Body.Close(); err != nil {\n\t\t\tapi.log.Warn(\"Failed to close response body\", \"error\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tapi.log.Info(\"Response received from loki\", \"status\", \"ok\", \"statusCode\", resp.StatusCode, \"contentLength\", resp.Header.Get(\"Content-Length\"), \"duration\", time.Since(start), \"contentEncoding\", resp.Header.Get(\"Content-Encoding\"), \"stage\", stageDatabaseRequest)\n\n\t// server errors are handled by the plugin-proxy to hide the error message\n\tif resp.StatusCode/100 == 5 {\n\t\treturn RawLokiResponse{}, readLokiError(resp.Body)\n\t}\n\n\tbody, err := io.ReadAll(resp.Body)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tapi.log.Debug(\"Error reading response body bytes\", \"error\", err)\n\t\treturn RawLokiResponse{}, err\n\t}\n\n\t// client errors are passed as a json struct to the client\n\tif resp.StatusCode/100 != 2 {\n\t\tlokiResponseErr := lokiResponseError{Message: makeLokiError(body).Error()}\n\t\tapi.log.Warn(\"Non 200 HTTP status received from loki\", \"error\", lokiResponseErr.Message, \"statusCode\", resp.StatusCode, \"resourcePath\", resp.Header.Get(\"Content-Encoding\"),\n\t}\n\n\treturn rawLokiResponse, nil\n}\n\nfunc getSupportingQueryHeaderValue(supportingQueryType SupportingQueryType) string {\n\tvalue := \"\"\n\n\t// we need to map the SupportingQueryType to the actual header value. For\n\t// legacy reasons we defined each value, such as \"logsVolume\" maps to the\n\t// \"logvolhist\" header value to Loki. With #85123, even the value set in the\n\t// frontend query can be passed as is to Loki.\n\tswitch supportingQueryType {\n\tcase SupportingQueryLogsVolume:\n\t\tvalue = \"logvolhist\"\n\tcase SupportingQueryLogsSample:\n\t\tvalue = \"logsample\"\n\tcase SupportingQueryDataSample:\n\t\tvalue = \"datasample\"\n\tcase SupportingQueryInfiniteScroll:\n\t\tvalue = \"infinitescroll\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\tvalue = string(supportingQueryType)\n\t}\n\n\treturn value\n}\n\n// setXScopeOrgIDHeader sets the `X-Scope-OrgID` header in the provided HTTP request based on the tenant ID retrieved from the context.\n// `X-Scope-OrgID` is needed by the Loki system to work in multi-tenant mode.\n// See https://github.com/grafana/loki/blob/main/docs/sources/operations/multi-tenancy.md\nfunc setXScopeOrgIDHeader(req *http.Request, ctx context.Context) *http.Request {\n\tlogger := backend.NewLoggerWith(\"logger\", \"tsdb.loki\")\n\n\tmd, ok := metadata.FromIncomingContext(ctx)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\t// Metadata are currently set and needed only locally for multi-tenancy, while on cloud\n\t\t// this is set by our stack\n\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Metadata not present in context. Header not set\")\n\t\treturn req\n\t}\n\n\ttenantids := md.Get(\"tenantid\")\n\tif len(tenantids) == 0 {\n\t\t// We assume we are not using multi-tenant mode, which is fine\n\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Tenant ID not present. Header not set\")\n\t} else if len(tenantids) > 1 {\n\t\t// Loki supports multiple tenant IDs, but we should receive them from different contexts\n\t\tlogger.Error(strconv.Itoa(len(tenantids)) + \" tenant IDs found. Header not set\")\n\t} else {\n\t\treq.Header.Add(\"X-Scope-OrgID\", tenantids[0])\n\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Tenant ID \" + tenantids[0] + \" added to Loki request\")\n\t}\n\treturn req\n}\n","numLines":371,"startLine":1,"totalLines":371}}}

46→func makeDataRequest(ctx context.Context, lokiDsUrl string, query lokiQuery) (*http.Request, error) {\n    47→\tqs := url.Values{}\n    48→\tqs.Set(\"query\", query.Expr)\n    49→\n    50→\tqs.Set(\"direction\", string(query.Direction))\n    51→\n    52→\t// MaxLines defaults to zero when not received,\n    53→\t// and Loki does not like limit=0, even when it is not needed\n    54→\t// (for example for metric queries), so we\n    55→\t// only send it when it's set\n    56→\tif query.MaxLines > 0 {\n    57→\t\tqs.Set(\"limit\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%d\", query.MaxLines))\n    58→\t}\n    59→\n    60→\tlokiUrl, err := url.Parse(lokiDsUrl)\n    61→\tif err != nil {\n    62→\t\treturn nil, backend.DownstreamError(fmt.Errorf(\"failed to parse Loki URL: %w\", err))\n    63→\t}\n    64→\n    65→\tswitch query.QueryType {\n    66→\tcase QueryTypeRange:\n    67→\t\t{\n    68→\t\t\tqs.Set(\"start\", strconv.FormatInt(query.Start.UnixNano(), 10))\n    69→\t\t\tqs.Set(\"end\", strconv.FormatInt(query.End.UnixNano(), 10))\n    70→\t\t\t// NOTE: technically for streams-producing queries `step`\n    71→\t\t\t// is ignored, so it would be nicer to not send it in such cases,\n    72→\t\t\t// but we cannot detect that situation, so we always send it.\n    73→\t\t\t// it should not break anything.\n    74→\t\t\t// NOTE2: we do this at millisecond precision for two reasons:\n    75→\t\t\t//  a. Loki cannot do steps with better precision anyway,\n    76→\t\t\t//     so the microsecond & nanosecond part can be ignored.\n    77→\t\t\t//  b. having it always be number+'ms' makes it more robust and\n    78→\t\t\t//     precise, as Loki does not support step with float number\n    79→\t\t\t//     and time-specifier, like \"1.5s\"\n    80→\t\t\tqs.Set(\"step\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%dms\", query.Step.Milliseconds()))\n    81→\t\t\tlokiUrl.Path = path.Join(lokiUrl.Path, \"/loki/api/v1/query_range\")\n    82→\t\t}\n    83→\tcase QueryTypeInstant:\n    84→\t\t{\n    85→\t\t\tqs.Set(\"time\", strconv.FormatInt(query.End.UnixNano(), 10))\n    86→\t\t\tlokiUrl.Path = path.Join(lokiUrl.Path, \"/loki/api/v1/query\")\n    87→\t\t}\n    88→\tdefault:\n    89→\t\treturn 97→\t}\n    98→\n    99→\tif query.SupportingQueryType != SupportingQueryNone {\n   100→\t\tvalue := getSupportingQueryHeaderValue(query.SupportingQueryType)\n   101→\t\tif value != \"\" {\n   102→\t\t\treq.Header.Set(\"X-Query-Tags\", \"Source=\"+value)\n   103→\t\t}\n   104→\t}\n   105→\treq.Header.Set(\"X-Loki-Response-Encoding-Flags\", \"categorize-labels\")\n   106→\tsetXScopeOrgIDHeader(req, ctx)\n   107→\n   108→\treturn req, nil\n   109→}\n   110→\n   111→type lokiResponseError struct {\n   112→\tMessage string `json:\"message\"`\n   113→\tTraceID string `json:\"traceID,omitempty\"`\n   114→}\n   115→\n   116→type lokiError struct {\n   117→\tMessage string\n   118→}\n   119→\n   120→func makeLokiError(bytes []byte) error {\n   121→\tvar data lokiError\n   122→\terr := json.Unmarshal(bytes, &data)\n   123→\tif err != nil {\n   124→\t\t// we were unable to convert the bytes to JSON, we return the whole text\n   125→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%v\", string(bytes))\n   126→\t}\n   127→\n   128→\tif data.Message == \"\" {\n   129→\t\t// we got no usable error message, we return the whole text\n   130→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%v\", string(bytes))\n   131→\t}\n   132→\n   133→\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%v\", data.Message)\n   134→}\n   135→\n   136→// we know there is an error,\n   137→// based on the http-response-body\n   138→// we have to make an informative error-object\n   139→func readLokiError(body io.ReadCloser) error {\n   140→\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n   141→\t_, err := buf.ReadFrom(body)\n   142→\tif err != nil {\n   143→\t\treturn err\n   144→\t}\n   145→\n   146→\tbytes := buf.Bytes()\n   147→\n   148→\t// the error-message is probably a JSON structure,\n   149→\t// with a string-field named \"message\". we want the\n   150→\t// value of that field.\n   151→\t// but, the response might be just a simple string,\n   152→\t// this was used in older Loki versions.\n   153→\t// so our approach is this:\n   154→\t// - we try to convert the bytes to JSON\n   155→\t// - we take the value of the field \"message\"\n   156→\t// - if any of these steps fail, or if \"message\" is empty, we return the whole text\n   157→\n   158→\treturn makeLokiError(bytes)\n   159→}\n   160→\n   161→func (api *LokiAPI) DataQuery(ctx context.Context, query lokiQuery, responseOpts ResponseOpts) (*backend.DataResponse, resp.StatusCode/100 != 2 {\n   198→\t\terr := readLokiError(resp.Body)\n   199→\t\tres := backend.DataResponse{\n   200→\t\t\tError:       err,\n   201→\t\t\tErrorSource: 204→\t\tapi.log.Debug(\"Error received from Loki\", lp...)\n   205→\t\treturn &res, nil\n   206→\t} else {\n   207→\t\tlp = append(lp, \"status\", \"ok\")\n   208→\t\tapi.log.Info(\"Response received from loki\", lp...)\n   209→\t}\n   210→\n   211→\tstart = time.Now()\n   212→\t_, span := api.tracer.Start(ctx, \"datasource.loki.parseResponse\")\n   213→\tdefer span.End()\n   214→\n   215→\titer 219→\t\tspan.RecordError(res.Error)\n   220→\t\tspan.SetStatus(codes.Error, res.Error.Error())\n   221→\t\tinstrumentation.UpdatePluginParsingResponseDurationSeconds(ctx, time.Since(start), 224→\t}\n   225→\tinstrumentation.UpdatePluginParsingResponseDurationSeconds(ctx, time.Since(start), \"ok\")\n   226→\tapi.log.Info(\"Response parsed from loki\", \"duration\", time.Since(start), \"framesLength\", len(res.Frames), \"stage\", stageParseResponse)\n   227→\n   228→\treturn &res, nil\n   229→}\n   230→\n   231→func makeRawRequest(ctx context.Context, lokiDsUrl string, resourcePath
